### 知乎用户 杨洋 发表
    
5 月 12 日至 5 月 14 日，七国集团（G7）外长齐聚德国[万格尔斯](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E4%B8%87%E6%A0%BC%E5%B0%94%E6%96%AF&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551798362%7D)，举行了一场针对如何解决[俄乌冲突](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E4%BF%84%E4%B9%8C%E5%86%B2%E7%AA%81&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551798362%7D)以及粮食危机的会议。虽然此次会议重点讨论的是俄罗斯，但七国集团显然没有忘记中国。

此次会议中，G7 国家达成了许多共识，公报中大约有一半的内容是针对中国，总共提到中国 10 次、台湾四次与南中国海三次。

自[俄乌战争](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E4%BF%84%E4%B9%8C%E6%88%98%E4%BA%89&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551798362%7D)爆发后，西方就对俄罗斯进行了各种制裁，为了拉中国下水，他们多次施压中国要求站队西方，对俄罗斯进行谴责。中国作为五常国家之一，在此次俄乌战争中并没有选择站边，而是一直保持中立态度。

由于中国没有终止与俄罗斯的各项正常合作，所以俄罗斯可以通过与中国的正常贸易，从中国获取一些必要的生活物资。对于中俄之间的正常合作，西方恶意抹黑中国意图，有些媒体甚至诬蔑中国对俄罗斯进行了许多军事援助。

关于西方邀请中国参加[核军控谈判](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E6%A0%B8%E5%86%9B%E6%8E%A7%E8%B0%88%E5%88%A4&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551798362%7D)一事，中方早就表示无意参加，如果美国愿意将核武库削减至与中国同等水平，我们倒是乐于参加核军控对话。

除此之外，G7 会议还提到了台湾问题。

最值得注意的是，其探讨中国的部分，所用的专项标题却是 “台湾”，给人强烈“拉台抗中” 的印象，且极尽蔑中之能事，极为奇特。

在这一部分，先是谈到与中国合作，比如气候与疫情，随即开始抨击，从新疆到香港，还有不公平贸易与网络攻击等，不遗余力，之后就是支持台湾加入 WHO 与 WHA，此乃 G7 外长公报的首次。

台湾问题是中国一直都想解决的重大问题，虽然中国花费了许多精力，但由于一系列外界因素干扰，这一问题直到现在还没有彻底解决。

中国也希望能够通过和平的方式解决这一问题，但由于美国等西方国家的介入，想要和平解决这一问题，变得非常艰难。而这次 G7 集团要求中国和平解决这一问题，是害怕中国大陆趁着俄乌战争期间，突然对台湾地区 “发动军事行动”。

以中国目前的军事实力，短时间 “摧毁台湾地区的所有防御设施” 非常轻松。而且，中国也没有对外承诺过不会用武力方式解决台湾问题，这使得民进党当局与美国政府产生了许多担忧。虽然美国在军事上能够压中国一头，但美国因为[俄乌问题](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E4%BF%84%E4%B9%8C%E9%97%AE%E9%A2%98&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551798362%7D)，自己也忙得不可开交，这时候再想干预台湾问题是非常困难的。

很显然，美西方管太多了，正如俄罗斯联邦安全会议副主席梅德韦杰夫所说，G7 [外长会议](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E5%A4%96%E9%95%BF%E4%BC%9A%E8%AE%AE&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551798362%7D)是西方国家粗暴干涉中国内政的又一例证。

中国核力量始终维持在符合国家安全需要的最低标准，哪里来的 “惊人扩张”？

中国没有大幅扩张核武器库的计划，只是会根据国家自身安全来更新核武库，并且根据国际安全形势对自身核力量进行评估，看看是否充足。但美国方面仍然紧抓中国核武不放，还声称在过去两年的时间里，中国方面已经将核储备增加一倍。

顺便一提，即使我国不止一次地解释那些所谓的 “[发射井](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E5%8F%91%E5%B0%84%E4%BA%95&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551798362%7D)” 只是发电设施，但美国方面还是乐此不疲地炒作中国核武库固体燃料[洲际弹道导弹](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E6%B4%B2%E9%99%85%E5%BC%B9%E9%81%93%E5%AF%BC%E5%BC%B9&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551798362%7D)发射井在不断扩大。

一直想将我国拉上军控谈判桌的美西方，在核军控上又做了什么？

目前我国核武器数量不足 300 枚，但美国不仅坐拥世界第二大核武库，这拥核数量也是在我国的数十倍。然而极为好笑的是，作为拥核大国的美国并没有加入核军控的行列，而是在想着如何给[核力量](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E6%A0%B8%E5%8A%9B%E9%87%8F&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551798362%7D)松绑，而之前美国伙同英国帮助[澳大利亚](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E6%BE%B3%E5%A4%A7%E5%88%A9%E4%BA%9A&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551798362%7D)建造核潜艇，就是实打实的证据。

再者说，美西方步步紧逼，使得俄罗斯不得不拿出 “[核威慑](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E6%A0%B8%E5%A8%81%E6%85%91&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551798362%7D)”，这个时候美西方怎么又不顾全球安危了呢？

G7 外长无视客观事实，在中国内政问题上指手画脚，分明就是 “满纸荒唐言”。

### 知乎用户  SanArtist 发表
    
其实他们也玩不出什么新花样！

历史总是惊人的相似，目前的国际局势与[战国中后期](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E6%88%98%E5%9B%BD%E4%B8%AD%E5%90%8E%E6%9C%9F&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551730339%7D)何其相似。秦国是后发国家，在六国看来，秦国是野蛮落后的；商鞅变法，更是被六国看成是野蛮粗暴的操作。秦国历来被六国看做异端，他们会五国、六国伐秦，但是他们貌似统一行动，实则貌合神离，各怀鬼胎，他们永远不可能做到铁板一块。只要秦国坚持商鞅变法，做好自己的事，守住基本盘，在外交上做好连横，每次斗争到关键时刻，从六国里拉出一两个不坚定者，就能瓦解他们脆弱的合纵！

最终，无论他们怎么折腾，也翻不起大浪！

七国集团，是发达国家俱乐部，1970 年成立时占全球 GDP 的 62%。随着西方经济体系陷入危机和亚洲国家的崛起，七国集团 GDP 占全球比例下降到 45%。实力大不如前，影响力迅速滑落！

而中国则从 1970 年 GDP 占全球 3%，增长到 2021 年 GDP 占全球 18% 左右，预计到 2028 年左右，中国 GDP 将超过美国，中国实力快速增长，将迅速扩大中国的国际影响力！

[七国集团](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E4%B8%83%E5%9B%BD%E9%9B%86%E5%9B%A2&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551730339%7D)内部也是矛盾重重，他们从骨子里瞧不起黄皮肤的异类日本，拍个照片都能给忽略了！日本无论怎么想[脱亚入欧](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E8%84%B1%E4%BA%9A%E5%85%A5%E6%AC%A7&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551730339%7D)，但是国家是搬不走的，它本身还是个亚洲国家的事实是改变不了的。它是东亚[儒家文化圈](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E5%84%92%E5%AE%B6%E6%96%87%E5%8C%96%E5%9C%88&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551730339%7D)的一员，也一直想成为东亚一哥，可惜不是中央之国，一千多年来始终是中央帝国的[番薯](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E7%95%AA%E8%96%AF&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551730339%7D)！只是近代，趁着中央帝国沉睡之际，短暂的辉煌了一下而已，随着中央帝国的再次崛起，东亚秩序将恢复正常状态，别看日本现在反抗最激烈，最终也不得不接受！

### 知乎用户 飙车君 发表
    
旦大学美国研究中心教授张佳栋将这几年 G7 峰会的联合公报做了一个比较，从前年压根没有提到中国，到去年 4 次提及中国，再到今年变成 14 次，这一变化 “非同寻常”，说明七国集团对中国的关注明显上升，而且这种关注是全方位的。

具体来看，南海、涉台问题，以及在新疆和西藏地区的所谓 “人权” 问题，都成为 G7 成员国的发难对象。在公报中，G7 不仅强调了 “维持印太地区自由、开放的重要性”，对东海和南海情势表达了“严正关切”，还再次强调了“台湾海峡和平稳定的重要性”。路透社等外媒用“前所未有” 来形容这份公报对中国提出的“严厉批评”。

事实上，在是否要加大对华攻击调门的问题上，美欧的态度一开始并不一致。香港《南华早报》的报道指出，虽然公报中的许多批评词汇无疑是陈词滥调，但美国此前一直无法成功说服 G7 其他成员国在公报中用类似表述提及涉华议题。还有一位德国官员表示，今年 G7 轮值主席国德国最初反对在公报中采用强硬的口吻，但还是同意了最终的措辞。

### 知乎用户 骐骥说 发表
    
首先，南海问题成为 G7 成员国的发难对象。公报宣称，G7 重申保持一个 “基于包容和法治、自由且开放的”“印太” 地区，强烈反对任何单方面以武力或强迫手段改变现状并增加紧张局势的企图，“我们强调，中国在南海的广泛海洋主张没有法律依据”。

### 知乎用户  黑心萝卜 发表
    
上个月[七国集团外长会](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E4%B8%83%E5%9B%BD%E9%9B%86%E5%9B%A2%E5%A4%96%E9%95%BF%E4%BC%9A&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551604939%7D)发表涉华负面公报，中方当即就予以明确回应。然而七国集团罔顾中方严正立场和坚决反对，再次利用峰会公报鼓吹 “民主对抗威权” 叙事，粗暴干涉中国内政，攻击抹黑中国，煽动[对抗情绪](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E5%AF%B9%E6%8A%97%E6%83%85%E7%BB%AA&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551604939%7D)。这充分说明，七国集团无意在平等尊重基础上开展对话合作，而是抱守冷战思维，坚持意识形态偏见，基于 “小圈子” 利益搞“集团政治”。

香港事务纯属中国内政。香港回归 25 年来，香港居民依法享有的民主权利和自由得到充分保障。中国政府依据[中华人民共和国宪法](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E4%B8%AD%E5%8D%8E%E4%BA%BA%E6%B0%91%E5%85%B1%E5%92%8C%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%AA%E6%B3%95&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551604939%7D)和香港基本法治理香港。这几个国家自身[人权](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E4%BA%BA%E6%9D%83&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551604939%7D)劣迹斑斑，没有任何资格充当人权 “教师爷”，更无权把人权当做干涉别国内政的政治工具。他们借炒作涉疆、涉藏等议题攻击抹黑中国，只会让世人更加看清他们的[霸权](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E9%9C%B8%E6%9D%83&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551604939%7D)本质和虚伪面目。世界上只有一个中国，台湾是中国领土不可分割的一部分，台湾当局推行 “[台独](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E5%8F%B0%E7%8B%AC&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551604939%7D)” 分裂活动、美西方个别国家企图 “以台制华”，这是当前[台海](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E5%8F%B0%E6%B5%B7&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551604939%7D)和平稳定面临的最大威胁。中国有权利采取一切必要措施坚决维护国家[主权](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E4%B8%BB%E6%9D%83&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551604939%7D)和安全。中国一贯模范遵守《[联合国宪章](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E8%81%94%E5%90%88%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%AA%E7%AB%A0&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551604939%7D)》宗旨原则，是世界和平发展、地区安全稳定的坚定维护者。这与美国到处发动战争、动辄实施[非法单边制裁](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%8D%95%E8%BE%B9%E5%88%B6%E8%A3%81&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551604939%7D)形成鲜明对比。

七国集团成员享受全球化发展[红利](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E7%BA%A2%E5%88%A9&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551604939%7D)最多。他们本应对推进全球化、促进世界经济增长、解决全球经济金融难题承担特殊责任。然而，在国际社会处于抗疫和经济复苏的关键时期，七国集团非但不致力于团结合作，反而热衷于制造分裂对抗，毫无责任和道义可言！我还必须强调的是，七国集团人口只占世界总人口的十分之一。他们没有资格代表全世界，更没有资格把自身价值和标准作为国际通用价值和标准。

七国集团应该切实承担起应尽的责任，履行应尽的国际义务，维护真正的[多边主义](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E5%A4%9A%E8%BE%B9%E4%B8%BB%E4%B9%89&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551604939%7D)。他们应该停止搞双重甚至多重标准，停止人为制造对立和分裂，停止以任何形式攻击抹黑中国，停止以任何形式干涉中国内政！

Foreign and Security Policy

We reiterate the importance of maintaining a free and open Indo Pacific, which is inclusive and based on the rule of law. We [re-emphasise](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=re-emphasise&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551433027%7D) our support for ASEAN unity and centrality and commit to explore concrete cooperation in line with the ASEAN Outlook on the Indo Pacific. We remain seriously concerned about the situation in the East and South China Seas. We strongly oppose any unilateral [attempts](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=attempts&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551433027%7D) to change the status quo by force or coercion that increase tensions. We emphasise the universal and unified character of the United Nations Convention on the Law of the Sea (UNCLOS), and reaffirm UNCLOS's

important role in setting out the legal framework that governs all activities in the ocean and the seas. We stress that there is no legal basis for China's expansive maritime claims in G7 Leaders' the South China Sea. In this regard, we urge China to fully comply with the arbitral award of 12 July 2016 and to respect navigational rights and freedoms enshrined in UNCLOS. We urge all parties to resolve disputes over maritime claims through peaceful means consistent with international law and support using the dispute settlement mechanisms established by UNCLOS. We underscore the importance of peace and stability across the Taiwan Strait and encourage a peaceful [resolution](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=resolution&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551433027%7D) of cross-Strait issues.

In the context of our cooperation with the largest [economies](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=economies&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551433027%7D), including in the framework of the G20, it is necessary to cooperate with China on shared global challenges, in particular addressing climate change and biodiversity loss and other relevant multilateral issues. We continue to call on China to uphold its obligations under international law and to contribute to international security. We remind China of the need to uphold the principle of the UN Charter on peaceful settlement of disputes and to abstain from threats, [coercion](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=coercion&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551433027%7D), intimidation measures or use of force.

As Russia is waging its unjustifiable, [unprovoked](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=unprovoked&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551433027%7D) and illegal war against Ukraine, we call on China to press Russia to immediately comply with the legally binding order of the International Court of Justice of 16 March 2022 and to abide by the relevant resolutions of the UN General Assembly and stop its military aggression - and immediately and unconditionally withdraw its troops from Ukraine.

We call on China to honor its commitments made in the Sino-British Joint Declaration and the Basic Law, which [enshrine rights](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=enshrine+rights&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551433027%7D), freedoms and a high degree of autonomy for

Hong Kong.We remain committed to upholding fair and transparent competition in the global economy and strengthening international rules in this regard. With regard to China's role in the global economy, we are continuing to consult on collective approaches, also beyond the G7, to challenges posed by non-market policies and practices which distort the global economy. We will build a shared understanding of China's non-transparent and market-distorting interventions and other forms of economic and industrial directives. We will then work together to develop coordinated action to ensure a level playing field for our businesses and workers, to foster [diversification](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=diversification&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551433027%7D) and resilience to economic coercion, and to reduce strategic dependencies.

We are gravely concerned about the human rights situation in China. We will continue to promote universal values, including by calling on China to respect universal human rights and fundamental freedoms, including in Tibet and in Xinjiang where forced labour is of major [concern](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=concern&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2551433027%7D) to us.
